{\*\ftnsep\chftnsep}\pgndec\pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa100{\cf1\b\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs34\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
Intro}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
It all started with the Budget Crisis of 3119, when the Co-operative finally realised the scale of the overspend on the project to upgrade the old Faraway wormhole navigation system to the new Witchspace Beacon network. Gross financial mismanagement is hardly new to the Co-operative, or even (sadly) uncommon, but the Faraway fiasco was of an entirely different order of magnitude. This hole wasn't going to be filled with some budgetary offset and a bit of creative accountancy; somehow, the Witchspace Beacon network would have to start generating income.}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
The idea of charging a levy on all ships using Witchspace was briefly considered, then discarded as a) unpopular and, sadly, b) impossible. Fortunately, a solution was found: the Ad-X Corporation was prepared to pay handsomely for the right to station giant TeraScreen advertisements at the Witchpoint (and, in some larger systems, outside the main station itself).}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
It seemed like the problem had been solved. Unfortunately, the only systems prepared to accept unrestricted TeraScreen advertising were the Corporate States, the Democracies and the Confederacies. Dictatorships wanted to use the screens for their own purposes (usually, giant pictures of one Glorious Leader or another); the Communist worlds would have nothing but propaganda (and, indeed, have been working on a system of propaganda screens of their own); and the Multi-Government, Feudal and Anarchy worlds wanted a slice of the pie for themselves \u8211\'96 one far bigger than their downmarket demographic warranted.}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
In desperation, the Co-operative cast around for other possible revenue streams. The various member worlds of the wealthy Corporate State voting bloc had always bridled at Co-op restrictions on the classes and quantities of commodities exchanged at main system stations, demanding "Free Trade" instead. Other planets in the Co-operative, fearful that their own domestic economies would be overwhelmed by an arrangement that inherently favoured the rich and powerful, had always resisted such demands. But faced with the possible bankruptcy of the entire stellar trading network, a compromise was reached: in return for a regular rent on the local Witchpoint volume, the Co-operative would allow a number of independent trading posts to be set up in systems with sufficiently high levels of economic, cultural and political cohesion \u8211\'96 or, as some cynics have suggested, those systems with a big enough population to make the venture worthwhile.}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
Thus the Convenience Stores were born: franchise stations, based near the Witchpoint, offering goods and services to passing ships. Exempt from Co-op trade regulations, the Convenience Stores set about making money from every possible source. They are encrusted with advertising, and even the stations' defence craft \u8211\'96 cheap ex-Navy Sidewinders \u8211\'96 are plastered with logos and corporate sponsorship. Most controversially, controlled commodities \u8211\'96 slaves, narcotics and firearms \u8211\'96 are offered freely, and legally, for sale.}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
Within a Convenience Store, commerce moves at a rapid pace, and prices of even the most basic goods can fluctuate wildly. Some merchants, for commercial or ideological reasons, have abandoned the main system stations altogether; but cannier Commanders, balancing the reliable price index of the Co-operative against speculative capitalist bubble-blowing, can often exploit the feverish atmosphere of a Convenience Store to obtain impressive profits on relatively small quantities of goods.}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa40{\cf18\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
-}

\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa40{\cf1\b\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs34\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
Overview}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
Do you want spam with that?}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
This OXP adds a lot of variety to the Universe. Witch-point and navigation beacons are replaced with giant bill boards displaying adverts. Every set features 50 different adverts and also adds a different type of constore to the universe (Set A introduces the Pi-42 constore, Set B the Tescoo Ooxpress constore ect). A constore is a dockable commercial base which is added to the space lanes of most systems with a large population. Also from version 4 and above of this oxp each constore has its own security force, the ships of which are skinned in the colours of the store they protect, and billboards will occasionally appear in asteroid fields of Corporate Systems.}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
All ads made by different Oolite players for a more varied visual experience. . Note that your ads must be relevant to the world of Oolite and submitted as 256x128 pixel images. Also for ver 4 and above all the artwork on the constores is a contribution of different oolite players}

\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5

\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5

\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5

\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa100{\cf1\b\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs34\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
Installing and Playing}
\par \pard\plain \s0\ql\nowidctlpar\hyphpar0\ltrpar\cf1\kerning1\dbch\af6\langfe1081\dbch\af6\afs24\alang1081\loch\f3\fs24\lang2057\sl380\slmult0\sb0\sa120{\cf1\b0\kerning1\dbch\af7\langfe1081\dbch\af8\rtlch \ltrch\loch\fs26\lang2057\loch\f5\hich\af5
To play the OXP, unzip the download file. This will create a forlder "YOUR_AD_HERE.oxp" and also several folders named "YOUR_AD_HERE_SET_X.oxp". In order to have a functional installation of your ad here you need the primary folder ("YOUR_AD_HERE.oxp") and at least one set ("YOUR_AD_HERE_SET_A.oxp" for examble). The more folder sets you chose to install the more the variety of the ads, constores ect you introduce to the universe. Move the folders you want under the AddOns folder inside your oolite installation}

Scripts

Scripts/yah_ad_script.js 
"use strict";

this.name        = "yah_ad_script"; 
this.author      = "spara";
this.description = "Changes ads on billboards";

this.shipSpawned = function() {
  this.$ws = worldScripts["yah_ad_service"];
	var numberOfAds = this.$ws.$adPool.length;
  var numberOfBrokenAds = this.$ws.$brokenAdPool.length;
  //is the current billboard broken?
  if (Math.random() < numberOfBrokenAds/(numberOfAds+numberOfBrokenAds)) {
    //if yes, just set the texture once to a broken texture.
    this._changeAd(this.$ws._getBrokenAd());
  }
  else {
    //in not, set the first ad and start the timer.
    this._changeAd(this.$ws._getAd());
		this.$billboardTimer = new Timer(this, this._rotateAds, 0, 15);
    //this.$billboardTimer = new Timer(this, this._rotateAds, 0, 1);
  }
}

this._rotateAds = function() {
	if (ship) {
		this._changeAd(this.$ws._getAd());
	}
	else delete this.$billboardTimer;
}

this._changeAd = function(ad) {
	ship.setMaterials({"yah_billboard_ad.png": {
		diffuse_map: ad,
		illumination_map: "yah_billboard_illuminate.png",
		illumination_modulate_color: (255, 255, 0),
		emission_map: ad,
		emission_modulate_color: "darkGrayColor"
	}});
}
Scripts/yah_ad_service.js 
"use strict";

this.name        = "yah_ad_service"; 
this.author      = "spara";
this.description = "Pooling ad service";

this.$adPool = [];
this.$brokenAdPool = [];

//public function for adding horizontal ad to pool. the parameter is the filename of the ad.
this._setAd = function(ad) {
  this.$adPool.push(ad);
}

this._setBrokenAd = function(ad) {
  this.$brokenAdPool.push(ad);
}

this.startUpComplete = function() {
  if (this.$adPool.length > 0) {  
    //shuffle the pool
    this.$adPool = this._shuffle(this.$adPool);
      
    //Pools are divided to two parts to prevent the same ad to be seen in a quick succession. Pools are split into two parts and a primary part is randomly selected. When the active part is emptied, then the secondary part is used. When that is emptied too, pool is initialized and we draw from the primary part again.

    this._initPool();
    this.$primary = Math.round(Math.random());
  }
  //in case no ad-packs are installed, always return a dummy ad.
  else this._getAd = this._noAds;
}

this._shuffle = function(pool) {
  var shuffled = new Array();
  var poolSize = pool.length;
  for (var i = poolSize; i > 0; i--) {
    shuffled.push(pool.splice(Math.floor(Math.random() * i), 1)[0]);
  }
  return shuffled;
}

this._initPool = function() {
	var poolSize = this.$adPool.length;
  this.$pool = [this.$adPool.slice(0, Math.floor(poolSize / 2)), this.$adPool.slice(Math.ceil(poolSize / 2), poolSize - 1)];
}

//public function that returns a random ad filename from the pool
this._getAd = function() {
  if (this.$pool[this.$primary].length === 0) {
    this.$primary = (this.$primary + 1) % 2;
    if (this.$pool[this.$primary].length === 0) {
      this._initPool();
    };
  };
  var adNum = Math.floor(Math.random() * this.$pool[this.$primary].length);
  return this.$pool[this.$primary].splice(adNum, 1)[0];
}

this._noAds = function() {
  return "yah_billboard_ad.png";
}

//public function that returns a random broken ad filename from the broken ad pool
this._getBrokenAd = function() {
  return this.$brokenAdPool[Math.floor(Math.random() * this.$brokenAdPool.length)];
}

Scripts/yah_constore.js 
"use strict";

this.name        = "yah_constore";
this.description = "ship script for constores";

this.shipSpawned = function() {
	//spawn a patrol (1-2 ships) around the station
	var count = 1 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 2);
	var shipdata = Ship.shipDataForKey(ship.dataKey);
	var defenseShip = shipdata["defense_ship_role"];
	var patrol = system.addShips(defenseShip, count, ship.position, 25E3);
	for (var i = 0; i < patrol.length; i++) {
		ship.group.addShip(patrol[i]);
		patrol[i].group = ship.group;
		patrol[i].switchAI("yah_patrolAI.js");
		patrol[i].forwardWeapon = "EQ_WEAPON_BEAM_LASER";
	}
}

//this makes the station behave very aggressively, if a ship in it's group is attacked
this.helpRequestReceived = function(ally, enemy) {
	//tame the behavior a bit
	if (Math.random() < 0.33) {
		ship.launchDefenseShip();
	}
}
Scripts/yah_market.js 
"use strict";

this.name = "yah-market";
this.author = "spara";
this.copyright = "2015 spara";
this.license     = "CC BY-NC-SA 4.0"; 

this.$originalDefs = {
      "food" : [0, 0, 22, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "textiles" : [0, 0, 22, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "radioactives" : [0, 0, 78, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "slaves" : [0, 0, 20, -4, -4, 20, 1, 2, 0],
      "liquor_wines" : [0, 0, 108, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "luxuries" : [0, 0, 235, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "narcotics" : [0, 0, 282, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "computers" : [0, 0, 185, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "machinery" : [0, 0, 140, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "alloys" : [0, 0, 94, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "firearms" : [0, 0, 149, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "furs" : [0, 0, 211, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "minerals" : [0, 0, 38, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0],
      "gold" : [0, 0, 65, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 1],
      "platinum" : [0, 0, 128, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 1],
      "gem_stones" : [0, 0, 34, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 2],
      "alien_items" : [0, 0, 80, -4, -4, 2, 1, 0, 0]
};

this.updateLocalCommodityDefinition = function(goodDefinition) {
	var commodity = goodDefinition.key;
	var oldDefs = this.$originalDefs[commodity];
	
	//this is a small market with extremely wacky prices and to respect the original author the market always has 10 items for sale.
	goodDefinition.capacity = 15;
	
	//old style definition found for the good. calculate it the old way
	if (oldDefs) {
		var market_base_price = oldDefs[2];
		var market_eco_adjust_price = oldDefs[3];
		var market_eco_adjust_quantity = oldDefs[4];
		var market_base_quantity = oldDefs[5];
		var market_mask_price = oldDefs[6];
		var market_mask_quantity = oldDefs[7];
		var market_rnd = Math.floor(Math.random() * 256);

		var economy = system.economy;
		
		var price = (market_base_price + (market_rnd & market_mask_price) + (economy * market_eco_adjust_price)) & 255;
		price *= 0.4;
		
		var quantity = (market_base_quantity + (market_rnd & market_mask_quantity) - (economy * market_eco_adjust_quantity)) & 255;
		if (quantity > 127) quantity = 0;
		
		quantity &= goodDefinition.capacity;//was 63
		
		goodDefinition.quantity = quantity;
		goodDefinition.price = price * 10;
	}
	//no definition found. just add some variance to the system market (+/-5%)
	else {
		goodDefinition.price = goodDefinition.price * (1.05 - Math.random() * 0.1);
		goodDefinition.quantity = Math.floor(goodDefinition.quantity * (1.05 - Math.random() * 0.1));
	}
	//scale down if quantity too high
	if (goodDefinition.quantity > goodDefinition.capacity)
		goodDefinition.quantity = Math.floor(goodDefinition.quantity / 127 * goodDefinition.capacity);

	//now we'll tame the market from producing too much profit.
	var maxProfit = 1000;//desicredits! How much profit is allowed for a single commodity when trading with the main station.
	var sPrice = system.mainStation.market[commodity].price;
	var priceDiff = goodDefinition.price - sPrice;
	//we'll make too much profit selling to the constore.
	if (priceDiff > maxProfit / goodDefinition.capacity) {
		//cap the quantity so that the possible profit won't go over maxProfit.
		var quantityMin = goodDefinition.capacity - Math.floor(maxProfit/priceDiff);
		//change the quantity only if needed.
		if (goodDefinition.quantity < quantityMin) {
			//recalculate quantity with flat distribution.
			var newQuantity = goodDefinition.capacity - Math.ceil(Math.random() * (goodDefinition.capacity - quantityMin));
			goodDefinition.quantity = newQuantity;
		}
	}
	//we'll make too much profit buying from the constore.
	else if (priceDiff < -1 * maxProfit / goodDefinition.capacity) {
		//cap the quantity so that possible profit won't go over maxProfit.
		var quantityMax = Math.floor(maxProfit/(-1 * priceDiff));
		//change the quantity only if needed.
		if (goodDefinition.quantity > quantityMax) {
			//recalculate quantity with flat distribution.
			var newQuantity = Math.ceil(Math.random() * (quantityMax));
			goodDefinition.quantity = newQuantity;
		}
	}
	return goodDefinition;
};
Scripts/yah_populator.js 
"use strict";

this.name        = "Pi-Forty-Two Con stores"; 
this.author      = "spara"; //heavily modified from the original by Ark.
this.copyright   = "2009 - 2016 the Oolite team."; 
this.description = "This script places constore stations near witchspace boys and also one asteroid billboard when the populator can not add at least one of them.";

this.$conStores = true;//spawn constores
this.$asteroidBillBoards = true;//spawn asteroid billboards
this.$noFuel = true;//block selling fuel at constores

this.systemWillPopulate = function() {
	if (this.$conStores && system.government > 0 && system.population > 40) {
		var conStores = Ship.keysForRole("constore");
		var conStoreInd = Math.floor(system.pseudoRandomNumber * conStores.length);
		var conStoreKey = conStores[conStoreInd];
		//add a little randomization to the position.
		var exactPosition = Vector3D(0, 5E3, -30E3).add([system.scrambledPseudoRandomNumber(321) * 8E3, system.scrambledPseudoRandomNumber(425) * 8E3, system.scrambledPseudoRandomNumber(847) * 8E3]);
		system.setPopulator("con_store", {
			callback: function(pos) {
				var addedShip = system.addShips("[" + conStoreKey + "]", 1, pos, 0)[0];
				addedShip.orientation = [1, 0, 1, 0]; // Orientate the side to the main planet for best view from the spacelane.
				var buoy = system.addShips("constore-buoy", 1, pos.add(addedShip.heading.multiply(10E3)), 0)[0];
				buoy.beaconLabel = addedShip.displayName;
			}.bind(this),
			location: "COORDINATES",
			coordinates: exactPosition,
			deterministic: true
		});
	}
	
	if (this.$asteroidBillBoards && system.government === 7) {
		var planetToSun = system.sun.position.distanceTo(system.mainPlanet.position) - system.sun.radius - system.mainPlanet.radius;
		var spawnFraction = Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.25;
		//this is just a rough position for the populator callback, inside I'll use addShipToRoute instead.
		exactPosition = Vector3D(0, 0, spawnFraction * planetToSun).fromCoordinateSystem("spm");
		system.setPopulator("con_store_asteroid_billboard", {
			callback: function(pos) {
				var billboard = system.addShipsToRoute("asteroid-billboard", 1, spawnFraction, 'sp')[0];
				system.addShips("asteroid", 8, billboard.position, 10E3);
				billboard.orientation = Quaternion.random();	
			}.bind(this),
			location: "COORDINATES",
			coordinates: exactPosition
		});		
	}
}

this.guiScreenChanged = function(to, from) {
	if (guiScreen === "GUI_SCREEN_EQUIP_SHIP" && player.ship.docked && player.ship.dockedStation.hasRole("constore") && this.$noFuel) {
		mission.runScreen({
			title: "Staff only",
			message: "Apologies for the inconvenience. Our shipyard is very small and its facilities are exclusively for our own needs.",
			background: "yah_no_entry.png"
		});
	}
}
